Use chicken yolk membrane or silk floss, baked dry and ground into powder. Apply dry if the area is moist, or mix with clear oil for application if dry.

**Abscess Opposite the Heart**
This abscess arises directly opposite the heart due to exuberant heart fire and the convergence of heat qi in this region. The toxin grows increasingly virulent and migratory. Urgent use of medicine to course and discharge heart fire is required, followed by flesh-generating remedies to achieve resolution.

**Honeycomb Abscess of the Chest**
This honeycomb abscess arises between the chest and breast due to exuberant heart fire. Treatment relies on the aforementioned medicine for coursing heart fire. Any delay risks the heat attacking the heart, resulting in certain death.

**Honeycomb Abscess of the Occiput**
This abscess arises at the back of the head in a honeycomb pattern. Urgent treatment is required. If it presents with redness, swelling, and pain, it is easily cured; if phlegm is involved, it becomes nearly incurable. Prompt oral and topical treatment is essential. Should it spread to both shoulders, it is absolutely incurable.

**Two-Headed Back Abscess**
If this abscess has two small heads with toxin spreading outward, it arises from dietary factors, where qi and food interact and combine due to deficiency. Qi deficiency causes dispersion, widening the opening. Urgent administration of medicine for internal resolution is required, along with yang supplementation.

**Abscesses and Flat Abscesses of the Flanks**
These abscesses and flat abscesses form beneath the flanks due to deficiency and qi vacuity. Under no circumstances should yang-supplementing medicine be administered. Since they arise from vacuity, hot formulas must be avoided; if heat is introduced, vacuity will worsen, and the heat will readily damage the bone membrane. Exercise utmost caution.

**Abscesses at the Hairline**
These abscesses arise at the hairline on either side of the nape. Urgent topical treatment is required. If they present as kernels, the root must be promptly excised. If they resemble brain-heart abscesses, heat qi ascends to attack the brain, causing redness, swelling, hardness, and pain around the ears and neck, accompanied by chills and fever. Without swift treatment, the toxin will enter the blood, causing flesh to rot and pus to form. If blood and qi emerge from the head, or if phlegm is involved, it is nearly incurable and fatal.

**Occipital Abscess**
This condition, called *Heavenly Flat Abscess*, presents as large and purplish-black. Without urgent treatment, heat will penetrate the armpit, injure the Conception Vessel, and internally scorch the liver and lungs, leading to death within ten days.

Apply the previously mentioned *Dissolve Toxin and Reduce Swelling Supportive Powder* and *Internal Support Thousand Gold Powder*, along with *Promote Flesh Growth and Relieve Pain* remedies to achieve efficacy.

**Postauricular Abscess**
This condition arises one *cun* and three *fen* behind the ear—a fatal location. If it develops, it is invariably fatal, hence termed *Acute Toxin* and left untreated. *Acute Toxin* presents as firm and sharply toxic, called *Mandibular Swelling*. When heat steams upward, connecting to the jaw and penetrating the mouth, it inevitably leads to throat perforation and death.

Prescribed remedies follow.

**Break Binding Powder**
Specifically treats *stone goiter*, *qi goiter*, *sinew goiter*, *blood goiter*, and similar conditions. Administer this remedy promptly, along with subsequent topical applications.
*Ingredients:*
- *Sargassum* (washed) – 3 *qian*
- *Gentiana* – 3 *qian*
- *Clam shell* – 3 *qian*
- *Rice-paper plant pith* – 3 *qian*
- *Fritillaria* (heart removed) – 3 *qian*
- *Kelp* (washed) – 3 *qian*
- *Alum* (calcined) – 3 *qian*
- *Usnea* – 3 *qian*
- *Wheat flour* – 1 *qian*
- *Pinellia* – 1 *qian*

Grind all into fine powder. Take half a *qian* per dose, mixed with warm southern wine. Avoid all toxic substances, licorice, chicken, fish, the five pungent vegetables, raw or cold fruits, and trees for efficacy.

**Arisaema Paste**
Specifically treats skin growths and tumors on the neck and face, ranging from fist-sized to millet-sized, whether soft or hard, painless or indolent. Apply this remedy—do not rashly use acupuncture or moxibustion. Instead, carefully puncture to release qi, then apply the paste.
*Ingredients:*
- One large *Arisaema* (finely ground until dry; add quality vinegar to form a paste. If fresh is unavailable, dried may be used—grind into powder and mix with vinegar to form a paste).

Puncture the growth slightly to allow qi to escape, then spread the paste on paper, cut to the size of the tumor, and apply. If itching occurs, do not scratch; reapply frequently for efficacy. When the paper dries, replace with a moistened application.

**Chest Abscess**
This condition, called *Well Abscess*, arises on the chest, resembling a large bean, and develops within three to four days. Without early treatment, it descends into the abdomen. If it enters the abdomen and remains untreated, death occurs within ten days. Urgently administer *Internal Consolidation and Clear Heart Powder* (formula as previously noted). External manifestations are treatable; internal penetration injures the membranes and is undoubtedly fatal.

**Nine Abscesses**
These include *lung abscess*, *heart abscess*, *liver abscess*, *kidney carbuncle*, *spleen abscess*, *stomach abscess*, *large intestine abscess*, *triple burner abscess*, and *small intestine carbuncle*. Examine the patient’s membranes, assess the abscess’s depth, determine the affected organ or bowel, and identify any prior consumption of mineral or stone medicines. Evaluate qi deficiency or excess—external perforation and drainage are treatable, while internal membrane injury with pus discharging through the stool is nearly incurable. Treat accordingly.

**Breast Abscess in Women**
For *breast carbuncle*, if occurring postpartum, it is called *external blowing*; if during pregnancy, *internal blowing*. Initially, apply topical powders for urgent treatment. If pus forms, use *Promote Flesh Growth and Relieve Pain* remedies for efficacy.

**Efficacy Powder**
*Ingredients:*
- *Angelica dahurica* – equal parts
- *Fritillaria* (heart removed) – equal parts

Grind into fine powder and take with southern wine. For blocked lactation, add *Rhaponticum* and decoct with wine for administration.

**Topical Remedy for Initial Breast Abscess and Internal/External Blowing**
Use one spoonful of yeast, mix with five *qian* of flour, stir-fry and grind until fermented dough resembles a beehive. Once fermentation turns the surface green, dry and grind into powder. Mix with well water and apply. If dry, moisten day and night. If unresolved, add *Angelica dahurica* and *Fritillaria* powder. For pain, add *Frankincense* and *Myrrh* powder for immediate efficacy.

For *breast carbuncle* and *breast abscess* with internal nodules that do not dissipate, urgently administer *Restore Origin and Unblock Qi Powder*, along with previously mentioned topical remedies, *Dissolve Toxin and Draw Out Toxin Powders*, and *Life-Saving Decoction* until sweating occurs.

**Restore Origin and Unblock Qi Powder**
Treats *breast abscess*, *breast carbuncle*, and all swelling toxins.
*Ingredients:*
- *Aucklandia* – equal parts
- *Fennel* – equal parts
- *Unripe tangerine peel* – equal parts
- *Pangolin scales* (roasted until crisp) – equal parts
- *Tangerine peel* – equal parts
- *Angelica dahurica* – equal parts
- *Licorice* – equal parts
- *Fritillaria* (ginger-processed, heart removed) – equal parts
- *Rhaponticum* – added

Grind all into powder and take with southern wine. Alternatively, decoct with water and add wine for administration.

**Alternative Formula**
*Ingredients:*
- *Unripe tangerine peel* – 1 *liang*
- *Tangerine peel* – 1 *liang*
- *Licorice* (raw and prepared) – 1 *liang*
- *Pangolin scales* (roasted) – 3 *liang*
- *Trichosanthes root* – 3 *liang*
- *Forsythia* – 1 *liang*
- *Honeysuckle* – 1 *liang*

Grind all into powder and take with hot wine.

**Breast Consumption**
Avoid needling, as injury to the mammary ducts is fatal. Identify the condition: if the mouth opens wide, the breast is damaged and decayed. Urgently administer remedies and apply topical treatments. Failure to promote flesh growth is fatal and untreatable. Administer *Secret Transmission Flow Qi Decoction* and *Supportive Ten Proclamations Powder*, with *Dissolve Toxin, Promote Flesh Growth, and Relieve Pain Powder* applied centrally, and the previous *blowing breast* topical remedy applied around the perimeter.

For *flowering* or *pomegranate* breast abscesses, these conditions are untreatable. Those aged thirty-two or thirty-three may be treated; those over forty should seek early treatment with oral and topical remedies. Failure to promote flesh growth renders the condition untreatable and fatal.

**Human Face Sore**
This condition arises from karmic retribution. Perform virtuous deeds to resolve it, with sincere repentance. Only then may remedies be applied. Administer *Flow Qi Decoction*; for chronic cases, take *Sophora Pill* to supplement kidney water. Apply *Dissolve Toxin, Promote Flesh Growth, and Relieve Pain Powder* for miraculous efficacy. Later, use plasters and flesh-promoting remedies to fill the sore.

**Sophora Pill**
*Ingredients:*
- *Sophora* – 4 *liang*
- *Saposhnikovia* – 1 *liang*
- *Schizonepeta* – 1 *liang*
- *Angelica dahurica* – 1 *liang*
- *Sichuan aconite* (raw, skin removed) – 1 *liang*
- *Red peony* – 1 *liang*
- *Fleeceflower root* – 1 *liang*
- *Ligusticum* – 1 *liang*
- *Notopterygium* – 1 *liang*
- *Gardenia* – 1 *liang*
- *Gleditsia* – 1 *liang*
- *Vitex* – 1 *liang*
- *Poria* – 1 *liang*
- *Dioscorea* – 1 *liang*
- *Tribulus* – 3 *liang*
- *Aconite* (stir-fried) – 3 *qian*
- *Astragalus* – 1 *liang*
- *Notopterygium* – 1 *liang*
- *Typhonium* – 1 *liang* (these four ingredients are called *Four Fresh Powder*; only 3 *qian* of *Aconite* is used)

Grind the above ingredients into a fine powder, mix with water and cooked wheat flour paste to form pills the size of *wutong* seeds. Take thirty to fifty pills per dose, two or three times daily, on an empty stomach, swallowed with warm southern wine. For those who do not drink wine, substitute with good tea. This tonifies Kidney Water.

**Chronic Outer Shin Sores**
For sores that persist for years without healing, this is often due to Kidney Water deficiency and downward collapse, or Spleen dampness overflowing. Take *Sophora Pill* to tonify Kidney Water, and apply *Toxin-Resolving, Flesh-Promoting, Pain-Relieving Powder*. Later, use *Interlayer Plaster*.

**Secret Transmission: Interlayer Plaster**
For chronic, long-standing shin sores that do not heal:
- *Old pine resin*
- *Camphor*
- *Milled lead* (stir-fried)
- *Water dragon bone* (i.e., ship’s red lime)
- *Calomel*

If unresolved, add:
- *Angelica dahurica*
- *Ligusticum*
- *Mantis egg-case*

Grind all into a fine powder. Melt the pine resin, add a small amount of clear oil, and mix. Prepare oil-paper bags according to the size of the sore, fill with the medicament, and bind over the wound after washing. Secure for two days; replace every four days.

Alternatively, decoct *Angelica dahurica*, *Ligusticum*, and *mantis egg-case* alone to wash the sore—also effective.

**Calf Abscess and Blood-Wind Sores**
For these two conditions:
- If an abscess or deep-rooted sore arises on the calf, those near the genitals or anus are difficult to treat; those on fleshy areas are easier to resolve.
- For men and women with *blood-wind sores* on the legs, if the condition flows downward, it is manageable; if it ascends to the hands, it is difficult to treat.

**Dorsal Foot Sores**
This condition arises from *wasting-thirst* (diabetes). When it appears on the toes, it is called *gangrenous detachment*. If the sore turns red-black, it is fatal and untreatable; if not red-black, it may be treated. If treatment fails to improve it, amputate immediately—this may save the patient. Failure to amputate will lead to red-black necrosis and certain death.

At onset, it may be treated: administer *Qi-Coursing Beverage*, *Sophora Pill*, and *Toxin-Resolving, Flesh-Promoting Medicines* with urgency. Another specific remedy: boil *tung oil* and *litharge* to a boil, add a spoonful of *Sichuan pepper*, and cut *water bamboo leaves* to fit the sore. Steep for seven days, then apply the leaves alone to the sore—this will resolve it. For sores on the fingers, use the same treatment.

**Kidney Yin Abscess**
This condition, called *suspended abscess*, manifests as swelling and pain on the scrotum. It arises when the Bladder and Kidney channels are affected by cold-damp *qi*, causing stagnation in the Yin meridians, blood and *qi* congealing, and cold-damp *qi* failing to disperse.

Administer the aforementioned *Supportive Wrapping Powder*, adding:
- *Plantago seed*
- *Akebia*
- *Bland bamboo leaf*
- *Morning glory*
- *Fleeceflower root*
- *Lotus stamen*

Also apply *Internal Dissipation Powder* and *Flesh-Promoting, Pain-Relieving Powder*, and cover with a plaster. Further, take the previously mentioned *Secret Transmission: Qi-Coursing Beverage*.

**Lower Abscesses**
*Secret Transmission: One-Ingredient Thousand-Gold Powder*—specifically for *scrofula*—works with miraculous efficacy. Use a single black spider (those that cross rivers are best), crush in a bowl, stir with hot southern wine, and consume in one draught. Lie on the side corresponding to the affected area. If unresolved, use another spider—this will be effective.

**Topical Medicines**
First, stir-fry scallion whites until hot and apply as a compress. If cooling occurs, reheat and apply three or four times. Then apply the medicine: use the aforementioned *Toxin-Transforming, Swelling-Reducing Medicine*, adding:
- *Garlic*
- *Momordica*
- *Arisaema*
- *Wild aconite*

For ruptured sores, use the aforementioned *Flesh-Promoting, Pain-Relieving Medicine*. Apply *Unblocking Medicine* three to five times as needed.

**Unblocking Medicine**
- *Morning glory*
- *Realgar*
- *Toosendan*
- *Rhubarb*
- *Licorice node*
- *Trichosanthes root*
- *Bitter orange*
- *Fritillaria* (equal parts)

Grind into powder. Take on an empty stomach with southern wine; discontinue once pus is discharged.

**Alternative Formula**
- *Asarum*
- *Coptis*
- *Pangolin scales*
- *Frankincense*
- *Myrrh*
- *Forsythia*
- *Tangkuei tail*
- *Rhubarb*
- *Gardenia*
- *Honeysuckle*
- *Oyster shell*
- *Plantago seed*
- *Saposhnikovia*
- *Licorice*
- *Oil walnut*

Chop, decoct in water until done, add southern wine, and take warm at dawn. For *unilateral Kidney qi*, this works with divine efficacy. First, take *Five-Ingredient Powder with Poria*, adding:
- *Virgate wormwood*
- *Rush pith*
- *Akebia*
- *White atractylodes*
- *Red poria*
- *Alisma*
- *Cinnamon*

Chop, decoct in water, and take on an empty stomach. Then apply moxibustion as described below for best results.

Later, take *Aucklandia Pill*: toast one dose with a large *blister beetle*, remove the beetle, and take with hot southern wine. If unresolved, take one or two more doses.

Another formula: decoct *chestnut tree root* in southern wine—this works immediately.

**Chancre Topical Medicine**
- *Coptis*
- *Phellodendron* (equal parts)

First, soak the two ingredients in the juice of two pig gallbladders until moist. Then place on a tile or brick heated over fire to dry. Add:
- *Frankincense*
- *Myrrh*
- *Mirabilite*
- *Calcined alum*
- *Litharge*
- *Chinese sumac gallnut*
- *Scorpion*
- *Sophora*

Grind into powder. For dry sores, mix with clear oil and apply; for damp sores, apply dry.

If swelling does not subside, use *Yiyuan Powder* with additions:
- *Saposhnikovia*
- *Schizonepeta*
- *Fleeceflower root*

Decoct in water and wash the area warmly.

For *chancre with persistent swelling*, use:
- *Saposhnikovia*
- *Schizonepeta*
- *Licorice node*
- *Achyranthes* (equal parts)

Decoct and use as a fumigant and wash—this will resolve it.

**Alternative Chancre Formula**
- *Litharge*
- *Coptis*
- *Phellodendron*
- *Calomel*

Grind into powder and apply. Wash with a decoction of salt and mugwort.

For oral medicine, pound *red kudzu root* and a piece of fresh ginger together, mix with hot wine, and consume until sweating occurs. Apply the dregs to the sore.

For *unilateral Kidney qi*, use the patient’s mouth as a measure: moxa above the navel—if the condition is on the left, moxa the right; if on the right, moxa the left. Then take one dose each of *Swift-Riding Fennel Pill* and *Evodia Internal Dissipation Pill*, swallowed on an empty stomach with raw wine and a pinch of salt.

**Swift-Life-Pursuing Decoction (Secret Formula, Rapidly Effective)**
This formula resolves swelling internally. Though already recorded in *Immortal-Transmitted External Medicine*, it is reproduced here for convenience of reference.

- *Notopterygium*
- *Pubescent angelica*
- *Green tangerine peel*
- *Saposhnikovia* (large dose)
- *Coptis*
- *Red peony*
- *Asarum*
- *Licorice node*
- *Cicada molting*
- *Silkworm* (stiff)
- *Rhizoma smilacis glabrae* (equal parts)

Add:
- *Human placenta*
- *Lycopus*
- *Honeysuckle*

If pus is present, add:
- *Fleeceflower root*
- *Angelica dahurica*

For purgation, add:
- *Aristolochia root*
- *Rhubarb*
- *Gardenia*
- *Morning glory seed*

For leg conditions, add:
- *Chaenomeles*

Prepare by cutting the ingredients. Each dose weighs five *qian*. For the first dose, add *lycopus leaf* and a small amount of *honeysuckle* (one *qian* each), along with one *liang* of fresh ginger. Pound together, then decoct with good wine and consume hot. For those who do not drink, decoct with water and a small amount of wine—this is also effective. Then decoct one and a half cups each of wine and water with ten slices of ginger, consume hot, and cover with clothing and bedding until sweating occurs. Once the condition improves, add two *qian* of *rhubarb* to the previous formula, decoct hot, and consume. Purging once or twice will eliminate residual toxins.

Though the formula’s ingredients may seem incongruous, repeated use has proven its efficacy without fail. If other symptoms arise, adjust the formula accordingly.

For vexation and vomiting, add one *qian* of *licorice node* and take with fermented bean curd water (ingredients above ground separately into powder).
For retching and nausea, add *frankincense* and take with *licorice* decoction mixed with bean powder. Alternatively, grind *purple lotus placenta* and old ginger with a mouthful of rice vinegar and consume.
For vexation and vomiting due to latent summerheat, use *Cinnabar Five-Ingredient Powder*.
For persistent retching, add *clove* and *lotus seed* to the previous decoction. If unresolved, use *Unchanging Metal Qi-Righting Powder* with *ginseng* and *costus root*.
For unceasing retching with cold limbs (termed "water-drinking"), take *Coptis and Elsholtzia Powder* with *Summerheat-Dispersing Pill*.
For cold hands and feet, use *chaenomeles* and *morning glory seed*.
For vexation, add *ophiopogon*, *red peony*, *gardenia*, and *rush pith*.
For tidal fever, add *bupleurum*, *scutellaria*, *bamboo leaf*, and *imperata root*.
For dim vision, add a small amount of *cinnabar*, *realgar*, and *musk*.
For abdominal distension, add *coix seed* and *calcium sulfate*.
For spontaneous diarrhea, add *white atractylodes*, *poria*, *nutmeg*, and *poppy husk*.
For unceasing abdominal pain, add *costus root* and *frankincense*.
For panting and cough, add *anemarrhena*, *fritillaria*, and a small amount of *rock sugar*.
For headache, add *ligusticum*, *angelica dahurica*, and *scallion white*.
For unceasing pain, pound *radish seed*, *ligusticum*, and *scallion white* and apply to the temples.
For copious phlegm and drool, pound fresh *mugwort* leaf tips with rice vinegar, extract the juice, and gargle to expel phlegm.
For sore throat, decoct *menispermum*, *mirabilite root*, *gardenia*, *bamboo leaf*, *mugwort*, and *rush pith* and gargle.
For constipation, use *red peony* (ginger-processed), *areca husk* (bran-fried), and *areca peel*.
For urinary retention, use *red peony*, *red poria*, *akebia*, *plantago seed*, and *rush pith*.
For bloody urine, use *rehmannia* and *plantago seed*.
For nosebleed, use *safflower*, *rehmannia*, *lotus rhizome node*, and *ginger peel* (fresh).
If the sore is painless and fails to rise, apply three cones of moxa. If it remains painless, the condition is incurable.
For steaming bones, add *imperata root*.
For absence of pulse, take *Twenty-Four-Ingredient Qi-Flowing Beverage*.

**Flying Dragon Life-Snatching Elixir**
Specifically treats *ding*-sores, *carbuncles of the back*, *brain abscesses*, *breast abscesses*, *bone-attaching abscesses*, and all headless toxic swellings and malignant sores. Upon consumption, a head will form; if painless, it will induce pain; if already formed, it will resolve immediately. This is the supreme treasure among remedies for malignant conditions—even in critical cases, it may be used without fail. Do not underestimate it.

- *Toad venom* (two *qian*, dried; dissolve in aged wine)
- *Dragon’s blood* (one *qian*)
- *Frankincense* (two *qian*)
- *Myrrh* (two *qian*)
- *Realgar* (three *qian*)
- *Calomel* (half a *qian*)
- *Chalcanthite* (one *qian*)
- *Musk* (half a *qian*)
- *Verdigris* (two *qian*)
- *Calcium sulfate* (one *qian*)
- *Cinnabar* (two *qian*, for coating)
- *Sea snails* (twenty-one, with shells)
- *Centipede* (one, wine-fried until yellow; remove head, feet, and brain; half a *qian*; omit if unavailable)

Grind all into fine powder, then grind the *sea snails* into a paste and mix with the previous ingredients to form pills the size of mung beans. If pills do not form, use wine-cooked flour paste. Each dose consists of only two pills. Have the patient chew three inches of *scallion white* until pulpy, then spit into the palm (left for men, right for women). Wrap the pills in the scallion and swallow with three to four cups of unfiltered hot wine. Rest in a draft-free area, covered with clothing and bedding. After the time it takes to walk five *li*, consume several more cups of hot wine to reinforce the medicine’s power. Profuse sweating is the desired effect. If sweating does not occur in severe cases, take two more pills. Sweating will then ensue, and the effect will be achieved. At the first sign of illness, two pills will resolve it; for severe cases of three to five days’ duration, take two more pills. If the *ding*-sore has *walked yellow* and reached the heart, it is difficult to treat. If cold sweats occur, the patient will die. If the patient cannot chew scallion, pound it and wrap the pills for swallowing with wine. For sores on the upper body, take after meals; for sores on the lower body, take before meals. After consumption, avoid cold water, cucumber, eggplant, oily noodles, pork, mutton, offal, fish, and all wind- and sore-provoking foods, as well as women’s laundry with fox odor. This remedy is infallible.

**Back Sore Formula**
- *Cephalonoplos* (one *liang*)
- *Oxalis* (half a *liang*)
- *Chinese angelica* (two and a half *qian*)
- *Frankincense* (one and a quarter *qian*)
- *Myrrh* (one and a quarter *qian*)

Dry by baking, grind into powder, and take seven *qian* per dose, mixed with hot wine.

If fresh herbs are available, grind them with wine and take warm, reserving the dregs to apply on the sore.

**For Lumbar Pain:**
Stir-fry black soybeans until hot, wrap in silk or cloth, and bind around the waist. Grind ginger into hot wine and drink until intoxicated, inducing sweating. If no sweat appears, repeat the process two or three times for certain efficacy.

**Cane Wound Formula:**
- *Hydrargyrum chloratum* (one *liang*)
- *Red halloysite* (one *qian*, raw)
- *Mercury* (one *fen*, pre-melted)

Grind the three ingredients with sesame oil into a paste, spread on umbrella paper, and apply to the wound, binding tightly. If the flesh is sunken, fill the cavity with this paste before applying for immediate effect. Also treats hemorrhoids and malignant tinea.

**Hemorrhoid Formula:**
- *Arsenic* (*xin*)
- *Licorice*
- *Alum* (raw)

Grind each into powder. In a bowl, layer *arsenic* powder first, then *licorice* powder, followed by *alum* powder. Calcine over fire, then repeat the layering and calcining three times. Sweep the resulting powder into a container, mix with cold water, and apply to the sore. Some pain is unavoidable; drink wine until intoxicated. By the next day, the sore will slough off.

**To Extract Boils:**
For any boil that does not emerge, use half a *Ba dou* kernel (shelled), grind with magnetite into powder, and mix with scallion saliva and honey into a paste. Apply to the sore, and the boil will emerge.

**For All Swellings and Toxins:**
Use ginger dough made from wheat flour and earth collected from the eastern side of a beam where it meets the ground. On a yang day, draw a circle (○) on the ground; on a yin day, draw a square (□). Dip ginger in fine rice vinegar and grind within the circle to collect earth. Place in a mortar, add *rhubarb* and *mirabilite* powder, and grind thoroughly with ginger. Apply to the toxic area, leaving the sore’s opening exposed; the toxin will discharge.

**Decaying Sores (Zhu Gan):**
Mix *calomel* and *Sháo fěn* for application. Also treats mild tinea.

**Scabies Formula:**
- *Hydnocarpus*
- *Coptis*
- *Licorice*
- *Oil walnut* (adjust quantity)
- *Elm bark*
- *Zanthoxylum*
- *Calomel*
- *Alum* (half raw, half calcined)
- *Cnidium*
- *Well-spring stone*

Grind each into powder, mix with oil walnut, and pound into a paste the size of a bullet. Wrap in coarse cloth and rub: for itching areas, scrub; for painful areas, press. The remedy takes effect upon application.

**Infantile Milk Tinea:**
Rub with *licorice powder*, then apply oil and soy paste.

**Acute and Chronic Convulsions:**
Administer a mouthful of clear water from a cold latrine pit for immediate cure.

*End of Scroll Nine of* **Immortal-Transmitted External Medicine Secret Formulas**

*Scroll Ten of* **Immortal-Transmitted External Medicine Secret Formulas**
*Compiled by Zhao Yizhen, the Yuanyang Master of Junyi*

**Treatise on Miscellaneous Conditions**

**Rescuing the Hanged:**
From dawn to dusk, even if the body is already cold, life may still be restored. If the region below the heart retains the slightest warmth, even after a full day, revival is possible. Immediately embrace the deceased to loosen the noose, remove the rope—*never cut it*. Gently adjust the throat to its proper position, lay the body flat, and cover with a quilt. Urgently blow into both ears through bamboo tubes. Have one person firmly grasp the hair without releasing, while stepping on both shoulders with the feet. Another should massage the chest and flex the limbs, kneading and stretching them. If revived, administer thin congee. This method revives all without fail.

**Rescuing the Drowned:**
First, pry open the drowned person’s mouth with a knife and place a chopstick horizontally between the teeth to allow water to drain. Alternatively, invert a jar or steamer, lay the drowned person’s abdomen over it, letting the head hang downward to expel water. If no jar or steamer is available, a round log may be used. After water is expelled, have a strong man carry the deceased on his back, with the legs draped over the shoulders, walking to force out all remaining water. Then, take a clod of wall earth, place it on the ground, and lay the drowned person supine upon it, covering the body with more wall earth—leaving only the mouth and eyes exposed. Naturally, the water’s qi will be absorbed into the earth, and the person may revive. Immediately blow alternately into the mouth, ears, nose, navel, and anus through bamboo tubes to restore the flow of qi between upper and lower. Also, insufflate a small amount of *pinellia* powder into the nostrils. If slightly revived, administer thin congee.

Another method from Sun Simiao for rescuing the drowned: urgently loosen the deceased’s clothing and sash, then apply moxa to the navel to revive.

**Rescuing Those Frozen in Winter After Falling into Water:**
If the limbs are cold, speech is lost, and only faint breath remains, do not immediately apply fire. Instead, fill a cloth bag with hot ashes and place it over the heart. Replace with fresh hot ashes as it cools. Once the eyes open, administer warm wine or rice broth.

**Rescuing Those Who Have Collapsed from Summer Heat:**
Do not expose to cold, for cold will cause death. Use warm water to continuously massage and wash the area between the heart and abdomen. If urgently needed on the road, place hot roadside earth over the abdomen and navel, and have someone urinate into the navel to revive.

**Rescuing Those Who Have Collapsed from Heatstroke and Thirst:**
Mash equal parts of hot roadside earth and garlic, mix with water, strain, and administer the liquid to revive.

**Rescuing Sudden Windstroke with Loss of Consciousness, Often Due to Phlegm Obstruction:**
Use two *qian* of raw *alunite*, ground into powder, and mixed with fresh ginger juice. Pry open the mouth and administer to induce drooling, either by vomiting or dissolution, to restore consciousness.

**Rescuing Sudden Collapse from Malevolent Qi with Loss of Consciousness:**
Grind leeks into juice and pour into the nostrils.

**Rescuing Those Who Appear Dead While Asleep:**
Drip leek juice into the nostrils. In winter, use leeks with roots, pound into juice, and administer.

**Treating Falls from Heights with Blood Stasis Attacking the Heart and Near-Death:**
Boil one large cup of *fermented soybean* in two bowls of water for three boils, strain, and administer. If the person suddenly loses breath and speech before the medicine can be prepared, pry open the mouth and pour in warm urine.

**For the Five Sudden Deaths—Crushed, Hanged, Drowned, Nightmare-Induced, or Postpartum Collapse:**
Use *pinellia* ground into a powder the size of a soybean and insufflate into the nostrils to revive instantly.

**Hua Tuo, the Divine Physician, said:**
Ten critical conditions strike as swiftly as wind and rain; thus, select these renowned formulas to rescue them.

**First Critical Condition: Cholera with Vomiting and Diarrhea**
Caused by cold drinks, exposure to cold, hunger, rage, or travel by cart or boat, which injures the stomach qi, leading to incessant vomiting and diarrhea, dizziness, blurred vision, muscle spasms, and cold limbs.
*Formula:*
- *Evodia* (half *liang*)
- *Chaenomeles* (half *liang*)
- *Fermented soybean* (half *liang*)

Stir-fry together until scorched. First, boil three *sheng* of water in an earthenware pot until bubbling, then add the three ingredients and decoct to two *sheng*. Administer in divided doses.
*Alternative Formula:* Use calcined *alunite* as powder; take one large *qian* per dose with boiling water.
*Another Formula:* Decoct one pinch of salt in one cup of vinegar to seven parts, and administer warm. Or decoct salted plums or other salty-sour substances for consumption.

**Second Critical Condition: Throat-Constricting Wind with Swelling, Pain, and Cold Limbs, Causing Immediate Qi Obstruction**
Use three pieces of *Gleditsia* husk, steep in one cup of water, and administer to cure instantly.
*Alternative Formula:* Grind one piece of *Gleditsia* husk with one *qian* of *soot from kitchen stoves* into powder, mix with cold water, add a few drops of clear oil, and administer.
*Another Formula:* Chop four *liang* of *cimicifuga*, decoct in four bowls of water to one bowl, and administer to cure.

**Third Critical Condition: Internal Injury with Hemoptysis**
Caused by excessive alcohol or sexual indulgence damaging the heart and lungs, leading to reckless movement of blood and qi, with bleeding from both mouth and nose.
*Formula:* Burn a handful of *schizonepeta*, place the ash on the ground to dispel fire toxicity, grind finely, and take three *qian* per dose with aged rice broth.
*Alternative Formula:* Grind *soot from kitchen stoves* finely, take three *qian* per dose with thick rice broth for three doses—excellent.

**Fourth Critical Condition: Arsenic Poisoning**
With restlessness, colicky pain in the heart and abdomen, dizziness, retching without vomiting, cyanotic complexion, and cold limbs.
*Formula:* Grind a handful of *indigo* finely and administer with well-drawn water.
*Alternative Formula:* Administer two *sheng* of sesame oil.
*Another Formula:* Take three bowls of *earth broth*—dig a hole in yellow earth, pour in water, stir until turbid, and administer.

**Fifth Critical Condition: Corpse-Like Syncope with Sudden Collapse, Loss of Consciousness, and Rumbling Qi in the Abdomen**
*Formula:* Mix half a cup of fresh ginger juice with one cup of wine, decoct until bubbling, and administer.

Still moxibust the *Dantian*, *Baihui*, and *Qihai* points.

**Sixth Critical Condition: Affliction by Ghostly Qi**
Sudden collapse, cold limbs, clenched fists, and bleeding from the nose and mouth.
*Formula:* Grind approximately one *qian* of *realgar* into powder and administer with a decoction of peach leaves.
*Alternative Formula:* Burn a well-worn undergarment—men use women’s clothing, women use men’s—into ash. Take two *qian* per dose with seven-boiling water.
*[Note: "触衣" refers to inner garments.]*

**Seventh Critical Condition: Yang Collapse**
Acute pain in the lower abdomen, retracted testicles, blackened complexion, panting, and spontaneous cold sweating.
*Formula:* Pound three stalks of scallion (with roots intact) in a stone mortar, decoct with five *sheng* of wine until reduced to two *sheng*, and administer in two doses. First apply heated salt to the *Qihai* point below the navel, ensuring the warmth is retained.

**Eighth Critical Condition: Ghostly Nightmare or Ghostly Assault**
Struck by a ghost in the bedchamber, making sounds and crying out without awareness.
*Formula:* Crush *zaoxintu* (hearth soil) into powder, take two *qian* per dose with freshly drawn water, and blow a half-fingernail’s pinch into the nostrils. Also moxibust the *Jumao* point between the big toes for twenty-one cones.
*Alternative Formula:* Decoct three seven-inch branches each of peach and willow (east-facing growth) in three bowls of water, and administer warm.

**Ninth Critical Condition: Breech Birth**
*Formula:* Grind seven *Sophora* seeds finely and administer with freshly drawn downstream water.
*Alternative Formula:* Burn one shed snake skin, fourteen cicada molts, and a lock of hair into ash, take in three doses with warm wine, and lie supine for a moment to facilitate delivery.
*Another Formula:* Prick the soles of the infant’s feet three to five times with a fine needle, then apply salt to the punctures to prompt proper delivery.

**Tenth Critical Condition: Retained Placenta**
Stagnant blood surging upward, causing delirium, with the placenta ascending.
*Formula:* Stir-fry one *sheng* of red adzuki beans, decoct in three *sheng* of water until reduced to two *sheng*, strain, and administer the liquid warm for immediate expulsion.
*Alternative Method:* Burn the woman’s own fingernails and toenails into ash, take with wine in one dose, then have a strong woman lift her while using a bamboo tube to press downward over the heart for efficacy.

**Prescriptions for Childbirth**
When a woman nears labor with lumbar and abdominal pain, do not hastily administer labor-inducing charms or drugs, nor allow her to squat prematurely. She should remain active and composed. If the infant is fully developed, it will emerge naturally when the qi is sufficient. Premature induction risks transverse or breech birth, leading to fatal complications—such self-inflicted harm is avoidable. Verified formulas follow.

**Purple Perilla Drink**
Treats all prenatal conditions in women. This formula both calms and induces labor, pacifying the fetus and regulating qi—its efficacy is profound and indescribable.
*Ingredients:*
- Purple perilla leaves, 1 *liang* (fire-dried)
- Areca peel, washed and dried, stir-fried with fresh ginger juice
- Ginseng, ½ *liang*
- Aged tangerine peel, ½ *liang* (remove pith, stir-fried)
- *Chuanxiong*, 8 *qian*
- Licorice, ½ *liang* (honey-fried)
- Northern white peony, 4 *qian* (lightly stir-fried)
- *Chuandanggui*, 1 *liang* (lightly stir-fried)

*Preparation:* Chop the ingredients. For each dose, decoct 3 *qian* with three slices of fresh ginger and a three-inch scallion stalk, and take on an empty stomach.
*For the seventh or eighth month of pregnancy:* Add ½ *liang* of *zhike* (soaked in rice water, stir-fried after removing the pith) and 3 *qian* of cardamom (stir-fried). Take once daily. At labor, decoct with downstream water.
*When labor pains begin in waves:* Grind a piece of high-quality *ruxiang* (frankincense) the size of a little finger into a thick paste with 1 *ge* of water, administer warm, and wait until the waters break before taking labor-inducing drugs.

**Labor-Inducing Formula**
*Ingredients:* One handful of *zuosheng* branches (one *chi* long, thoroughly washed) and a five-inch piece of licorice, both chopped.
*Preparation:* Decoct in seven bowls of water in an earthenware pot, seal tightly with paper, and simmer until reduced by half. When the mother’s labor pains intensify, administer one cup warm. No more than two doses are needed; a sensation of downward pressure signals imminent delivery.
*This formula also treats transverse or breech birth, retained stillborn fetus with putrefaction, or prolonged retention. Repeatedly verified.*
*Alternative Formula:* Mix equal parts *baicaoshuang* (soot from kitchen stoves) and *baizhi* into powder, knead with boy’s urine and a little vinegar into a paste, and administer with hot water.
*Another Formula:* Burn the wooden shavings from an axe’s eye (where the handle fits) to ash, and administer with swiftly flowing water.
*For retained placenta pressing against the heart:* Burn snake skin to ash, mix with a small amount of musk, grind finely, and administer with warm wine for immediate delivery.

**Retained Placenta**
*Formula:* Separate the whites from three eggs, mix with 1 *ge* of sour vinegar, and have the woman sip it to expel the placenta.
*Alternative Method:* Have the woman hold the end of her own hair in her mouth to induce retching, prompting expulsion.
*Another Formula:* Peel and grind fourteen castor beans, apply the paste to the soles of her feet, and the placenta will descend. Wash off immediately. If the uterus prolapses, apply the same paste to the crown of the head to retract it. This remedy is harmless if used repeatedly; wash off once the uterus returns.

**Postpartum Blood Surge**
When stagnant blood rushes upward, causing blood faint (resembling sudden death), decoct aged mugwort in water with vinegar and administer.

**Uterine Flooding**
*Formula:* Grind *huangqin* into powder, take 2 *qian* per dose with wine heated by a red-hot iron scale weight.
*Alternative Formula:* Burn lotus seedpods to ash, take 2 *qian* per dose with wine.
*Another Formula:* Burn cotton, palm fiber, and hair to ash, mix with *baicaoshuang*, grind into powder, and administer with ash-free wine.

**Jiyin Elixir**
Treats all women’s ailments.
*Ingredients:*
- *Xiangfuzhi* (nutgrass)
- Black soybeans
- Dried ginger
- *Cangzhu* (atractylodes)

*Preparation:* Weigh four *liang* of each. Soak in aged vinegar for two seven-day periods (*cangzhu* for one seven-day period), then slice. Soak again for one seven-day period, remove the soybeans, and stir-fry.

Crush *xiangfuzhi* (nutgrass), add 1 *liang* of *danggui* (Chinese angelica) and ½ *liang* of *zhuyu* (evodia fruit), boil in vinegar, then dry-fry together and grind into powder. Form into pills the size of *wutong* seeds with glutinous rice paste. Take 20–30 pills on an empty stomach with warm wine or vinegar decoction. Indications follow those in the *Formulary*.

**Detoxification for All Poisons, Febrile Disorders, and Miscellaneous Ailments**
*Resolving All Poisons and Foodborne Toxins*
Use 2 *liang* of *gancao* (licorice), cut fresh, decoct in 3 cups of water until reduced by half, strain, and cool. Take ½ cup at a time, sipping slowly. If ineffective, repeat; vomiting is harmless.
*Alternative Formula:* Decoct with black soybeans for enhanced efficacy.

*Resolving All Poisons and Fujian-Guangdong "Peach-Born Gold Silkworm" Gu Toxins*
Use 49 stems of *gancao*, each 7 inches long, soak in a latrine for 49 days, wash clean, grind into powder, and store in a honey-sealed jar. When poisoned, chew in the mouth to resolve.

*Resolving Pi Toxin*
Burn early-harvest rice straw to ash, strain the juice through silk with freshly drawn water, and take 1 bowl cold. Toxin will descend with diarrhea, restoring stability.
*Alternative Formula:* Take *baibiandou* (white hyacinth bean) powder with freshly drawn water.
*Another Formula:* Decoct *qingdai* (indigo), *gancao*, and black soybeans in 3 bowls of water and administer.
*Another:* Force-feed a thick decoction of fermented soybean paste.
*Another:* Grind water from a tin vessel on a coarse stone and administer; water ground from tin is especially effective.
*Another:* Decoct 2–3 bowls of *yangmei* (bayberry) bark and administer.

*Resolving Death from Drug Poisoning*
If only the heart remains warm, the condition is treatable—this results from heat-afflicting substances.
Use *fangfeng* (saposhnikovia) alone, grind in cold water, and administer.
*Alternative Formula:* Grind *baibiandou* flowers in water.
*Another:* Mix bean starch with water, rice malt sugar with water, or grind fresh ginger in water and administer.

*Resolving Shumang Toxin*
Grind *mulan* (indigo) roots in water and administer several bowls.
(Also known as *ranqing* roots.)
*Another Formula:* Grind *wujiu* (Chinese tallow tree) roots in water and administer. Or grind *jingmiancao* (pilea) into its natural juice, mix with 1 small cup of wine and an equal portion of clear oil, stir well, and administer. The toxin will descend 3–5 times; follow with meat congee without delay.

*Resolving Badou (croton) Toxin*
Decoct *huanglian* (coptis) and administer the juice.

*Resolving Monghan (knockout) Toxin*
Drink cold water to restore stability.

*Resolving Gu Toxin*
Use *shichangpu* (acorus) alone, dry-fry, grind into powder, and administer with a *gancao* decoction until the condition resolves.

**Immortal-Transmitted Gu Toxin-Resolving Incantation**
When entering a household afflicted by *gu* toxin, recite the incantation silently 3 or 7 times upon arrival:
*"Father is an earthworm,
Mother is a silk-robed serpent maiden,
With seven thousand kin—
I know all of you."*
Upon entering, silently greet the *gu* toxin with a bow, then raise your gaze from the left hand straight upward, counting the roof rafters once before lowering your head. If offered tea, wine, or food, stealthily pluck a single pubic hair with your left hand, place it on the plate, and return it to the host. Silently recite the incantation 3 times as before. If a poisoned plate is present, creatures will emerge—tie them with the hair to identify the afflicted host.

*Alternative Formula: Filth Powder*
Have the patient chew a piece of *baifan* (alum). If it tastes sweet, *gu* toxin is present. Then collect filth from comb teeth, regardless of quantity, and ingest to induce vomiting of foul matter.

*Resolving Fuzi, Chuanwu, and Tianxiong Toxins*
Decoct black soybeans (large or small) and administer the juice.

*Resolving Banmao (blister beetle) Toxin*
Administer the juice of black soybeans (large or small). Grinding *yuzan* (plantain lily) roots in water also resolves various toxins.

*Resolving Wild Mushroom Poisoning*
Dig a pit in yellow earth, pour in cold water, stir until turbid, and drink after settling. Called "earth broth," it resolves all such toxins.
*Alternative Formula:* Decoct *gancao* nodes (any quantity) once in 1 cup of sesame oil, ensuring it does not blacken or cool, and administer the oil.

*Resolving River Pufferfish Poisoning*
In emergencies without medicine, urgently force-feed copious clear oil to induce vomiting of the toxin, restoring health.

**Detoxification Powder**
For any ingested poison, induces vomiting of worms with divine efficacy.
Use equal parts *baifan* (alum) and *shichangpu* (acorus), grind into powder, and take 2 *qian* with freshly drawn water. Two doses yield results.

**Immortal’s Detoxification Pill Formula**
- *Qingdai* (indigo)
- *Zirantong* (pyrite)
- *Ye cigua* (wild *cigua*, field-grown)
- *Guanzhong* (dryopteris)
- *Chuanxiong* (ligusticum)
- Wall dust
- *Huanglian* (coptis)
- *Taogen* (peach root bark removed, core dried and ground separately)
- *Binglang* (areca nut)
- *Chixiaodou* (red adzuki bean)
- *Lüdou* (mung bean)
- New bricks
- New tiles (must be unused and unexposed to water; soak in a latrine for 2 seven-day periods, then in flowing water for another 2 seven-day periods, dry, and grind separately)

Weigh 2 *liang* of each of the above 13 ingredients, plus 1 *liang* of *gancao* nodes. Grind into powder, mix with water ground from a tin vessel, then knead with glutinous rice paste cooked to a thick consistency. Pound 3,000 times to form pills the size of a bullet, testing doneness by floating in water when boiled with iron. Administer with water ground from tin.

**Divinely Bestowed Taiyi Powder**
Treats both yin and yang patterns of febrile disorders, effective for undifferentiated exterior-interior conditions.
- *Chuanshengma* (cimicifuga)
- *Baishaoyao* (white peony)
- *Zisuye* (perilla leaf)
- *Gange* (pueraria)
- *Chenpi* (aged tangerine peel)
- *Chuanxiong* (ligusticum)
- *Qingpi* (green tangerine peel)
- *Gancao* (licorice)
- *Xiangfuzhi* (nutgrass)
- *Baizhi* (angelica)

Grind equal parts into powder. Take 3 *qian* per dose, decoct in 1½ cups of water with 3 slices of fresh ginger until reduced to 80%. Administer two consecutive doses.
For headache, add 3 stalks of *cong* (scallion) with roots.
For qi stagnation and abdominal fullness, add *zhiqiao* (bitter orange).
Safe for postpartum women, infants, and the elderly, with divine efficacy.

**Treating Febrile Chest Bind**
Use 7 inches of *dahuanglian* (rhubarb) and 14 shelled *badou* (croton seeds).

Grind the above into powder, mix with saliva to form a small cake, place in the navel, and apply moxa cones atop it. Cease when heat penetrates the abdomen, regardless of the number of cones used. After moxibustion, wipe the area with a warm, damp cloth to remove toxins. This method has repeatedly saved lives.

**Treating Malaria**
Take 7 *qian* of *haochangshan* (dichroa root) and 3 *qian* of *binglang* (areca nut). Grind into fine powder, mix with egg white, and form into pills the size of *wutong* seeds. Take 30 pills per dose with warm wine or vinegar decoction. Administer once the night before onset and again at dawn on the day of onset—highly effective. For chronic cases, increase dosage to achieve results.

Another method: Slice *changshan* (dichroa root), mix thoroughly with egg white, steam over rice three times, discard the egg white, dry the *changshan* in the sun, grind into powder, and form into pills with cooked rice. Take 20 pills before bed and at dawn with wine—cures without inducing vomiting or diarrhea.

Another remedy: *Qinghao* (sweet wormwood) and *bo gui* (thin cinnamon bark), each ground into powder. For predominantly cold malaria, use more cinnamon and less wormwood; for predominantly hot malaria, use more wormwood and less cinnamon. Pound 2 *liang* of fresh ginger (with skin) to extract juice, mix with hot wine, and consume. Cover with blankets and rest to recover.

Another method: Regardless of chronic or recent onset, highly effective. Take 1 *liang* of *changshan* (dichroa root), thin as chicken bones, chop, soak in good vinegar overnight, then cook in an earthenware vessel until dry. Grind into powder, take 2 *qian* per dose, decoct in 1 cup of water until reduced to half, strain, and cool. Administer at dawn—divinely effective without inducing vomiting or diarrhea.

Another remedy: Equal parts *zhimu* (anemarrhena), *beimu* (fritillaria), *changshan* (dichroa root), and *binglang* (areca nut). Chop, decoct in equal parts water and wine until reduced to half, strain, cover with silk, and expose to dew overnight. At dawn, consume cold while facing east. Effective for all types of malaria, even chronic cases unresponsive for years—relief after one dose. However, women must not prepare the decoction.

**Treating Red and White Dysentery**
Take 6 *hezi* (chebula fruit), roast 6 until cooked and use 6 raw. Remove pits, dry the flesh, and grind into powder. For red dysentery, take with a decoction of raw *gancao* (licorice); for white dysentery, take with a decoction of roasted *gancao*. Administer on an empty stomach—severe cases require no more than two doses.

**Dysentery Pills**
Take 2 large *banxia* (pinellia), 7 shelled *badou* (croton seeds), 1 *qian* of *baicaoshuang* (soot from burned herbs), and 1 piece of *jingmo* (ink stick) the size of *banxia*. Grind all into powder, mix with 3 *qian* of yellow wax and a small amount of clear oil, and form into pills the size of mung beans. Take 7 pills per dose: for red dysentery, with *gancao* (licorice) decoction; for white dysentery, with *ganjiang* (dried ginger) decoction; for tenesmus, with *zhiqiao* (bitter orange) decoction; for food stagnation and cold-induced diarrhea, take cold with *ganjiang* decoction; for summer heat diarrhea, take with cold boiled water. Divine efficacy beyond description.

**Treating Aphthous Dysentery**
This condition may be cold, hot, or a mix of both. First disperse exterior and interior conditions. If palms are hot and eyes red, it is heat—use *Baidu San* (Antiphlogistic Powder) with *chenmi* (aged rice) decoction. If palms are cold and pure white dysentery occurs, it is cold—grind *lianrou* (lotus seed, with heart intact) into powder, mix with rice water, and take 3 *qian* per dose. Once able to eat, treat according to cold or heat symptoms.

Another remedy: Use *hongmujin* flowers (without stems), dry in shade, and grind into powder. Prepare two wheat flour pancakes, sprinkle the flower powder on top, and consume. Before eating, force the mouth open with water to administer the powder.

Another remedy for heat dysentery: Equal parts *chaihu* (bupleurum) and *huangqin* (scutellaria). Decoct in half water and half wine until reduced to 70%, cool, and take on an empty stomach or in the morning. For bloody dysentery, increase *huangqin*.

Another remedy: Remove the pit from 1 *wumei* (mume fruit), mix with fine spring tea powder, and take with vinegar decoction.

**Treating Cramping Diarrhea**
Decoct *chen’ai* (aged mugwort) and *mugua* (chaenomeles) in water, add a small amount of vinegar, and take a pinch.

Another method: Decoct 3 *qian* of *wuzhuyu* (evodia) with mugwort in 1½ cups of water, divide into three doses—immediately effective.

If herbs are unavailable, simply decoct *aiye* (mugwort) and fresh ginger together and take hot.

**Treating Intestinal Colic (Sha Syndrome)**
Onset causes unbearable abdominal pain. For *yin sha* (cold colic), the abdomen hurts and limbs are cold. Locate red spots on the body and burn them with an oil-dipped rush wick. For *yang sha* (hot colic), the abdomen hurts and limbs are warm. Prick the back of the fingers near the nails (about 1.5 *fen*) where the skin moves—bleeding brings relief. First, massage both arms downward to gather stagnant blood at the fingertips for bleeding.

If pain is unbearable and risks death (anciently called "dry cholera"), urgently dissolve 1 *liang* of salt in hot water and pour into the patient’s mouth—relief comes when salt reaches the abdomen.

Another remedy: Stir-fry stones until red, quench in cold water, and drink 1–2 *ge* of the clear liquid.

Another remedy: Equal parts *chenzhangmu* (aged camphor wood), *chenpi* (aged tangerine peel), and *chenbitutu* (aged wall earth). Decoct thickly, strain, and take 3–4 consecutive doses for relief.

**Treating Cholera with Vomiting and Diarrhea (Unresponsive to Other Medicines)**
Grind 49 *lüdou* (mung beans) and 49 *hujiao* (black peppercorns) into powder, decoct in water, and take. For severe thirst, grind into fine powder and take with fresh well water—divinely effective.

**Treating Uncontrollable Cholera Diarrhea**
Decoct 1 handful of fresh *ai* (mugwort) in 2 cups of water until reduced to 1 cup, and take all at once. If fresh mugwort is unavailable, use a thick decoction of aged mugwort leaves.

Another remedy: 1 *liang* of *mugua* (chaenomeles), ½ *liang* of *zhuyu* (evodia, soaked in hot water seven times), 2 *qian* of *huixiang* (fennel), and 2 *qian* of *gancao* (licorice). Chop, take 4 *qian* per dose, decoct in 1½ cups of water with 3 slices of ginger and 10 *zisu* (perilla) leaves. Take on an empty stomach.

**Moxibustion Method for Early-Stage Carbuncles and Back Boils (Repeatedly Tested and Verified)**
At the first sign of a carbuncle or back boil—whether already formed or not—if there is redness, heat, swelling, and pain, cover the area with damp paper and observe where it dries first; this marks the head of the boil. Slice a large garlic clove into pieces the thickness of a *dang* coin (approx. 3 *qian*), place one slice on the head, and apply moxibustion with three *zhuang* of mugwort. Replace the garlic slice and continue moxibustion: if painful, moxa until pain ceases; if painless, moxa until pain arises. Early detection and prompt moxibustion yield the best results. For boils present one or two days, ten moxibustions cure ten cases; for three or four days, six or seven cures; for five or six days, three or four cures. After seven days, moxibustion is no longer effective. If multiple heads cluster in one area, grind garlic into a paste, form a cake, place it over the boil heads, and burn mugwort atop it—this will also bring relief. If a red swelling on the back contains a yellow kernel like a millet grain, slice a single garlic clove and apply moxibustion as above; the next day, remove the scab, and the pus will have already discharged.

**Bamboo Tube Suction Method for Toxins (Effective for All Malignant Sores)**
Select a section of bitter bamboo one to two *cun* long, preferably with a node at one end. Scrape the green outer layer until paper-thin, adjusting the tube’s size to match the sore. Best used at the onset of toxic sores.
**Ingredients:**
- *Baijili* (white caltrop) – 5 *qian*
- *Cangzhu* (atractylodes) – 5 *qian*
- *Wujupi* (Chinese tallow tree bark) – 5 *qian*
- *Houpo* (magnolia bark) – 5 *qian*

Chop the four ingredients, decoct with the bamboo tube in one *diao* of water until the medicine is exhausted. While the tube is hot, press it onto the sore; soon, it will adhere on its own without manual pressure. Prepare another tube with the same proportions of medicine. When the first tube cools, remove it and replace it with a hot one, repeating the process. The pus will be drawn into the tube, and the sore will heal.

**Tenfold Diffusion Powder for Carbuncles and Boils**
All carbuncles and boils arise from stagnation of qi and blood, obstruction by wind-toxins. This formula disperses wind-evil, promotes the flow of qi and blood, drains pus, relieves pain, generates flesh, and closes wounds. For unformed sores, it swiftly dissipates them; for formed sores, it hastens suppuration. Without testing the five toxins, one may still achieve efficacy.
Master Xu states: Once, a patient with a back sore failed to heal with various medicines. This formula was administered—five to six *qian* dissolved in one *sheng* of warm wine. Shortly after, the pain diminished by seventy percent. After several doses, the sore suppurated, and within half a month, the wound closed. Another case involved a woman with a bowl-sized swelling on her thigh, which resolved with this treatment. A patient with a cranial boil took the medicine, drank to intoxication, and slept; upon waking, the ailment was gone. The key lies in selecting high-quality ingredients and administering ample doses. Continue taking the medicine even after the wound closes to replenish prior depletion and prevent future recurrence. For those who do not drink, it may also be taken with a thick decoction of *muxiang* (costus root), though a small amount of wine is preferable.

**Ingredients:**
- *Renshen* (ginseng, preferably from Silla) – remove the root head, finely chop, and dry-fry
- *Danggui* (Chinese angelica, large Sichuan variety resembling a horse’s tail) – wash thoroughly, slice, and dry-fry
- *Huangqi* (astragalus, silky variety, unbranched like an arrow shaft over a *chi* long) – wash, cut into *cun* sections, crush, split into strands, soak in saltwater until saturated, then gently roast until supple, and slice
- *Chuanxiong* (Sichuan lovage, high-quality) – wash, slice, and dry-fry
- *Fangfeng* (saposhnikovia, freshly fragrant) – wash, slice, and dry-fry
- *Houpo* (magnolia bark, thick and purple) – remove coarse bark, soak in ginger juice overnight, then stir-fry and dry-fry
- *Gancao* (licorice)
- *Jiegeng* (platycodon, with a bitter-tasting core) – wash, remove root head, slice, and dry-fry
- *Baizhi* (angelica dahurica)
- *Rougui* (cinnamon, thinly rolled) – remove coarse bark, avoid fire exposure

Take the first nine ingredients in their purest, driest form, weigh, and grind into powder. *Renshen*, *danggui*, and *huangqi* each use two *liang*; the remaining seven ingredients each use one *liang*. Add *rougui* and blend evenly. Dosage: three *qian*, increasing to five or six *qian*. Purchase ample *rougui*, remove impurities, and weigh the pure powder. With sincere preparation and generous dosing, efficacy is assured.

**Yellow Wax Pill for Back Boils, Carbuncles, and All Malignant Sores**
A patient with sores resembling snake heads covering the body also found relief with this remedy.
Use any amount of raw *baifan* (alum), grind into powder, and for every *liang* of alum, melt seven *qian* of yellow wax (remove from heat before mixing). Combine evenly and form into pills the size of *wutong* seeds. Dosage: ten to twenty or thirty pills, taken at any time with rice water or warm boiled water. For unruptured sores, it resolves them internally; for ruptured sores, it promotes closure. Typically, efficacy is achieved within ten or so doses. For sores caused by mineral or metal drug toxicity, this remedy is also suitable. Alternatively, take one to two spoonfuls of raw alum powder with warm water—equally effective. Use mountain wax, yellow in color, for best results. This formula does not disturb the viscera, relieves pain, and is safe for the elderly, weak, or infirm. It powerfully protects the membranes, rescues the heart, and prevents heat-toxin from attacking internally, averting critical danger. Its wonders are beyond description.

**Oak Leaf Decoction for Back Boils and Carbuncles (Formed or Unformed)**
Simple, inexpensive, and ideal for aiding the poor.
**Ingredients:**
- Dried oak leaves – 4 *liang*
- Dried lotus leaf heart and stem – 1 *liang*
- *Xuancaogen* (daylily root) – 1 *liang*
- *Gancaojie* (licorice nodes) – 1 *liang*
- *Diyu* (burnet) – 1 *liang*

Chop into a powder. Dosage: half a *liang* per serving, decoct in two bowls of water until reduced to half a bowl, and divide into two doses. Take morning and evening until the condition resolves. For formed sores, it promotes suppuration; for unformed sores, it induces resolution. Avoid all toxic foods.

**Additional Remedy for Carbuncles and Boils**
Grind *jilongying* leaves (from a chicken coop) into a paste, add a small amount of *guan* (salt), and apply, leaving the boil head exposed—immediately effective.

**Treatment for Scrofula (Regardless of Ruptured or Unruptured)**
Pierce the top of a black chicken egg, stir the yolk and white evenly, then tie a *banmao* (blister beetle) with string—removing its head, wings, and legs—and insert it into the egg. Seal with paper, steam over rice, peel the shell, remove the beetle, and consume the egg on an empty stomach, one per day, until healed.

**Additional Remedy**

Bundle thirty uninfested *zaojiao* (Chinese honey locust pods) together, wrap in palm fiber, and bind securely. Soak in a latrine pit for one month, then transfer to flowing water for another month—never use stagnant water. Remove the palm fiber, dry in the sun (do not bake), and grind into fine powder. For each *liang* of *zaojiao* powder, add half a *qian* of *shexiang* (musk) and seven whole scorpions; grind finely and blend evenly. Take two *qian* per dose, mixed with warm wine or water as preferred. Recovery typically occurs after consuming no more than two to three *liang*.

**Treatment for Nail-like Sores (Dingchuang)**
For unruptured *dingchuang* (nail-like sores), where the poison risks entering the intestines and stomach, use *chantui* (cicada moltings) ground into powder. Mix half a bowl with honey water and drink, and apply the powder mixed with saliva to the sore—its opening will naturally rupture.

**Alternative Remedy**
Take three or four *wumei* (dark plums), remove the flesh, mash, and bind tightly over the sore with silk. Then crush *juhua* (chrysanthemum) leaves, stems, and roots with wine and drink; for those who do not drink, use a decoction. By the following evening, remove the plum—the sore will have ruptured.

**Another Remedy**
Grind fresh honey with year-old scallions into a paste. First pierce the sore, then apply the paste, securing it with cloth. After the time it takes to walk five *li*, the *ding* (core) will emerge; wash it away with hot vinegar water.

**Treatment for Chronic Leg Sores (Lianchuang)**
Grind *xuexie* (dried lac insect resin) into powder and apply to the sore until dry.

**Alternative Remedy**
Grind *gudan* (realgar-processed lead) and *wumingyi* (pyrolusite) finely, mix with clear oil, and apply. If the sore is damp, dust the powder directly.

**Secret Remedy**
Grind well-fired yellow earth from a kiln into fine powder, then blend with *huangbo* (phellodendron bark), *chishizhi* (halloysite), *huangdan* (lead oxide), and *qingfen* (calomel) powders. Mix with clear oil, place in oiled silk, and apply to the sore, securing it with cloth. Even if the sore itches, do not disturb it with the hands. Leave in place for several tens of days until the sore heals, then remove.

**Treatment for Stubborn Sores and Scabies**
Grind equal parts *xionghuang* (realgar), *liuhuang* (sulfur), *huanglian* (coptis), *shechuangzi* (cnidium seed), and *jiandaocao* (sheargrass), then dry-bake. Fry seven *badou* (croton seeds) in sesame oil until black, discard the seeds, and once the oil cools, add high-quality *qingfen*. Mix with the prepared powder and apply.

**Palm-Rubbing Powder (Hezhang San) for Various Scabies and Leprous Sores**
Grind one and a half *liang* of *madouling* (birthwort fruit) into powder. Separately grind two and a half *qian* of *baifan* (alum) and three *qian* of *liuhuang* (sulfur). Blend evenly with clear oil, rub onto the hands, warm by rubbing, and inhale the vapor through the nose—the sores will resolve.

**Treatment for Malignant Sores Resembling Plums, Apricots, or Small Beans**
Grind one *liang* of *wuzhuyu* (evodia fruit) with two *liang* of *xiaosuan* (garlic) and apply. Change three times daily until improvement.

**Treatment for Long-Standing Unhealed Sores**
Dry-bake *dongguaye* (winter melon leaves), grind into powder, and apply—repeatedly effective.

**Treatment for Breast Abscess (Ruyong)**
Burn one *qian* of *shetui* (snake slough) to ash, mix with half a *qian* of roasted *gancao* (licorice), and take with warm wine. For ruptured abscesses, apply the powder with fresh oil.

**Alternative Remedy**
Burn *zaojiao* (Chinese honey locust pods) to ash, blend with *bengfen* (clam shell powder), and take with wine, massaging the breast to disperse the swelling.

**Alternative Remedy**
Burn *zongzhu* (reed leaves used for wrapping zongzi) collected on the fifth day of the fifth lunar month to ash, mix with wine, and drink—repeatedly effective.

**Another Remedy**
Crush *mabiancao* (verbena) with wine, stir-fry until brittle, and add a piece of ginger. Drink one or two bowls while hot, then apply the dregs to the affected area.

**Treatment for Water-Damp Sores (Shuihengchuang)**
Remove the kernel from one *zhizi* (gardenia fruit), insert a piece of *baifan* (alum), and roast in fire. Grind the entire mixture (including the shell) into powder and apply to the sore. First wash the sore with water before applying the powder.

**Treatment for Gan Sores (Ganchuang)**
Calcine *lugaoshi* (calamine) with fire, quench in vinegar, and grind into powder. Mix with oil and apply; adding *xiangcha* (fragrant tea) or *hai’erni* (child’s clay) enhances the effect.

**Alternative Remedy**
Crush fresh *yinxing* (ginkgo nuts) and apply. Also effective for pubic lice.

**Alternative Remedy**
Mix *huangbo* (phellodendron bark) with egg white, stir-fry three to five times, grind into powder, and blend with clear oil. For damp sores, dust the powder directly.

**Another Remedy**
Burn one whole *ganlan* (olive) to ash, mix with oil, and apply.

**Treatment for All Sores on the Head**
Boil an egg yolk until fully cooked, then stir-fry to extract its oil. Blend the oil evenly with *qingfen* (calomel) and apply. **Alternative Remedy:** Take one dose of *Pingwei San* (Calm the Stomach Powder), mix with *qingfen*, and blend with clear oil before applying.

**Treatment for Mouth Sores**
Grind equal parts *gancao* (licorice root) and *baifan* (alum) into powder and hold in the mouth to dissolve. **Alternative Remedy:** Crush *wuzhuyu* (evodia fruit), mix with vinegar, and apply to the soles of the feet. **Another Remedy:** Grind *wubeizi* (gallnut) into powder and dust onto the sores. **Another Remedy for Heat in the Triple Burner Causing Intolerable Pain from Mouth and Tongue Sores:** Grind equal parts *poxiao* (mirabilite), *wuweizi* (schisandra fruit), *huashi* (talc), *huangbo* (phellodendron bark, honey-toasted), *baifan* (calcined alum), *huangdan* (lead oxide, stir-fried), *hanshuishi* (calcined glauberite), and *xuanhusuo* (corydalis rhizome) into powder. Dust onto the sores; healing occurs swiftly.

**Treatment for All Swellings, Toxic Sores, and Carbuncles (to Promote Healing if Ulcerated or Resolve if Not)**
Grind *caowu* (wild aconite) into fine powder, mix with *jinghua shui* (well water drawn at dawn), and apply to the swollen area, leaving the sore’s head uncovered. Do not apply to broken sores. Adding *furongye* (cotton rose leaf) enhances the effect.

**Treatment for Kidney Wind (Itchy Scrotum with White Hands)**
Roast a pig’s scrotum over fire until cooked, and consume on an empty stomach with warm wine. **Alternative Remedy:** Wrap *zaojiao* (Chinese honey locust) in glutinous straw, burn to produce smoke, and fumigate the affected area ten times or more for healing. Take *Qingxin Lianzi Yin* (Lotus Seed Drink to Clear the Heart) as an oral remedy.

**Treatment for Creeping Snake Cinnabar Rash**
Grind *zaoxintu* (hearth ash) to powder, mix with clear oil, and apply. **Alternative Remedy:** Chew glutinous rice flour with salt and spit onto the affected area. **Another Remedy:** Grind a rusty iron nail with water and apply. **Another Remedy:** Pound *malandan* (horse orchid) with vinegar and apply for immediate healing.

**Treatment for Intolerable Pain and Foul Odor from Snake-Head Finger**
Bake one *wugong* (centipede) until dry, grind into powder, mix with pig bile, and apply. **Alternative Remedy:** Grind raw *heidou* (black soybeans) into powder, place inside a *zhizi* (gardenia) husk, and bind to the fingertip for relief.

**Treatment for Eyebrow Sores**
Take five or seven fresh pig leg bones, split open, and extract the marrow. Melt *tongyao* (copper rust) into the marrow, then gradually add *baijiaoxiang* (resin) powder while stirring to form a paste. Remove, place on a new brick to dispel fire toxicity for one hour, grind into powder, and mix with *qingfen* (calomel) in proportion to the number of bones. Blend with oil for application; dust dry powder onto damp sores.

**Treatment for Throat Conditions**
Boil *chuanshengma* (black cohosh) weighing one *liang* in one bowl of water. Hold the decoction in the mouth for about an hour before swallowing. Three doses will cure. **Alternative Remedy:** Calcine *baifan* (alum), place on the ground briefly to dispel fire toxicity, then hold in the mouth to dissolve.

**Treatment for Throat-Binding Wind**
Finely chop one plump *zaojiao* (Chinese honey locust), remove the seeds, soak in one large cup of water, grind, and strain to obtain a thick juice. Add a mouthful of raw hemp fibers, stir well, and consume in one dose. Frequently stir the throat with a goose feather to induce vomiting of saliva. Follow with wind-toxin-resolving medicinals. **Alternative Remedy:** Grind *baiyao* (white medicinal powder) with vinegar, hold in the mouth, and spit out toxic saliva.

**Treatment for Double Tongue**
Grind raw *baifan* (alum), *gudan* (processed lead oxide), and *wubeizi* (gallnut) into powder, mix with honey, and apply to the tongue. After a short while, rinse with water and reapply until healed. **Alternative Remedy:** Apply a small amount of *puhuang* (cattail pollen) to the tongue for immediate resolution.

**Treatment for Swollen, Hard Tongue Causing Suffocation and Distress**
Mix equal parts *baicaoshuang* (soot from burned herbs) and *shijian* (food residue) with *jinghua shui* (well water drawn at dawn) and apply to the tongue for healing. **Alternative Remedy for Throat Obstruction and Double Tongue:** Grind *poxiao* (mirabilite) and *baifan* (alum) into powder and dust into the mouth. **Another Remedy:** Grind *danfan* (chalcanthite) with good vinegar, hold in the mouth, and spit out saliva.

**Treatment for Reversed Stomach**
Reversed stomach is a fatal condition in nine out of ten cases, unresponsive to medicine. The error lies in forcing food or broth, which hastens vomiting. The correct approach is to avoid forcing food or broth. First administer *Laifu Dan* (Return Again Elixir) for summerheat; if not a summerheat pattern, then use *Yangzheng Lingsha* (Spirit Sand to Nourish the Upright) and similar remedies. When hungry, dry-fry rice until fragrant and consume without any liquid. After three days, vomiting ceases, and normal eating resumes. **Prescription:** Pound seven *sheng* (1.4 liters) of sugarcane juice and one *sheng* (200 ml) of fresh ginger juice, mix, and divide into three doses. **Alternative Remedy:** Remove the pit from one *zaozi* (jujube), wrap one whole *banmao* (blister beetle) inside, and roast over gentle fire until done. Discard the beetle, consume the jujube on an empty stomach with plain hot water. **Another Remedy:** Drink one cup of *lüniao* (donkey urine) daily.

**Nine Immortals Cake for Reversed Stomach**
- *Renshen* (ginseng): 2 *qian*
- *Nanmuxiang* (costus root, unheated): 2 *qian*
- *Gancao* (licorice root): 1 *qian*
- *Nanxing* (arisaema, washed seven times in ginger juice): 2 *qian*
- *Banxia* (pinellia, washed seven times in ginger juice): 5 *qian*
- *Zhiqiao* (bitter orange peel, stir-fried with bran): 1 *liang*
- *Baifan* (alum, calcined until crisp): 1 *liang*
- *Douchichi* (fermented soybean, calcined): 1 *liang*
- *Houpo* (magnolia bark, soaked in ginger juice and stir-fried): 5 *qian*

Prepare each ingredient according to the specified method, grind into fine powder, and expose to dew on a clear night. Use a decoction of *renshen* and *houpo* to form cakes the size of small coins. Dry over low heat. For each dose, take one cake, place between two slices of fresh ginger, wrap in paper, moisten, and roast over gentle fire until fragrant. Chew the cake with the ginger, and swallow with a decoction of authentic *Pingwei San* (Calm the Stomach Powder). Strictly avoid all raw and cold foods. Ensure the patient remains relaxed and optimistic; only then will the treatment be effective.

**Treatment for Chronic Reversed Stomach Unresponsive to Medicine and Persistent Infantile Vomiting**
Grind ½ *liang* of fine *liuhuang* (sulfur) and mix with 2½ *qian* of *shuiyin* (mercury) until no mercury specks remain. For each dose, take 3 *qian*, mix with hot wine and fresh ginger juice, and consume on an empty stomach. Gradually add wine while stirring to ensure even blending. After taking, cover with a blanket to induce sweating.

**Divine-Efficacy Powder for Wasting-Thirst**
White peony root and roasted licorice root, equal parts. Grind into a coarse powder. For each dose, take 3 *qian*, decoct in 1½ cups of water until reduced to 80%, strain, and consume. No fixed time; take thrice daily. Discontinue when the condition resolves.

**Divine-Efficacy Pills for Wasting-Thirst**
2 *liang* of *mituoseng* (litharge) and 1 *liang* of *huanglian* (coptis rhizome, rootlets removed). Grind into a fine powder, mix with steamed-cake paste to form pills the size of *wutong* seeds. Swallow with a thick decoction of silkworm cocoon skins, salted water, wine, or eggplant-root decoction. Start with 5 pills on the first day, increasing by 5 pills daily up to 30 pills. Do not exceed this dosage. Discontinue when thirst subsides.

There was once a traveler at an inn afflicted with this ailment who, unable to obtain water at night, drank the liquid from a pot and recovered. Upon inspection the next morning, it was found to be silkworm cocoon decoction.

**Alternative Formula**
Burn the wooden peg from a bull’s nose until carbonized, retaining its properties. Grind into powder and take with wine, or slice and decoct in water. Several doses will prove effective.

**Treatment for Urinary Retention**
Decoct *wujiumu* (Chinese tallow tree bark) and take with *Wuling San* (Five-Ingredient Powder with Poria). The flow will be restored immediately. Where no medicine is available, a decoction of the bark alone will suffice.

**Alternative Formula**
9 *qian* of *jingjie* (schizonepeta) and 1 *qian* of *dahuang* (rhubarb). Decoct and consume. Effective.

**Treatment for Constipation and Wind-Induced Obstruction in the Elderly**
Burn aged *zaojiao* (Chinese honey locust) until carbonized, retaining its properties. Cover with a bowl overnight. Take on an empty stomach with wine; the bowels will move immediately. Alternatively, grind *luofuzi* (radish seeds) and take with cold water to restore flow.

**Alternative Formula**
9 *qian* of *dahuang* and 1 *qian* of *jingjie*. Decoct in water and consume on an empty stomach. Effective.

**Treatment for Urinary and Fecal Retention Lasting Three to Five Days**
Burn undamaged *zaojiao* until carbonized. Take 5 *qian* mixed with rice-water decoction. Effective.

**Treatment for Blood in Urine**
Gather ample *cheqianzi* (plantain) roots and leaves, wash thoroughly, and extract the juice. Consume frequently to resolve the five types of strangury.

**Treatment for Gravel Strangury with Unbearable Pain**
Take one nine-lobed turtle shell, roast until crisp, and grind into powder. Take one spoonful with wine, repeating until effective.

**Alternative Formula**
Wash a handful of *tuniuxi* (local achyranthes) thoroughly, decoct in 5 cups of water until reduced to 1 cup, and strain. Add a small amount of *shexiang* (musk) and *ruxiang* (frankincense), grind finely, and consume.

**Alternative Formula**
120 black soybeans and a 1-*cun* slice of *gancao* (licorice). Decoct in fresh water, add 1 *qian* of *huashi* (talc) while hot, and consume on an empty stomach.

**Treatment for Blood Strangury, Often Resulting from Deficiency and Debilitation**
For each 5 *qian* dose of *Pingwei San* (Calm the Stomach Powder), add 1 *qian* of *longgu* (dragon bone) and decoct. Consume on an empty stomach. Several doses will prove effective.

**Alternative Formula**
Burn *baimei* (dried plum) until carbonized, retaining its properties. Grind into powder, add a small amount of *shexiang*, and form into *tongzi*-sized pills with wine paste. Swallow 50 pills with warm water.

**Treatment for Cloudy Urine and Frequent Turbid Discharge**
Roast aged winter melon seeds and grind into powder. Take approximately 5 *qian* with rice-water decoction on an empty stomach. Frequent doses will prove effective.

**Alternative Formula**
4 *liang* of *baifuling* (white poria) and 1 *liang* of *zhuling* (polyporus). Decoct in 1 bowl of water until reduced by half, discard the *zhuling*, and dry the *fuling*. Grind into powder, melt beeswax, and form into pills the size of bullets. Chew 1 pill thoroughly each morning and swallow with a decoction of *dengxin* (rush pith), *zaozi* (jujube), and *maimendong* (ophiopogon). Alternatively, take *Bi Xie Fen Qing Yin* (Dioscorea Hypoglauca Decoction to Separate the Clear).

**Treatment for Chronic Spleen-Induced Diarrhea**
4 *liang* of fresh ginger and 1 *liang* of *huanglian*. Slice both, stir-fry over low heat until the ginger is dry and deep red. Discard the ginger and grind the *huanglian* into powder. For each dose, take 2 *qian* with tea on an empty stomach. Alternatively, the aforementioned Yellow Wax Pills will also prove effective. *(See Abscess and Carbuncle Formulas.)*

**Treatment for Edema**
Boil black soybeans to remove their skins, dry, and grind into powder. Take 2 *qian* per dose with rice-water decoction.

**Push-Cart Pills for Jaundice and Edema**
½ *jin* of wheat flour, 2 *liang* of *mingfan* (alum), and 1 *liang* of *qingfan* (melanterite). Stir-fry together until red, then form into pills with vinegar-cooked rice paste. Take 30 pills with jujube decoction.

**Alternative Formula for Jaundice**
1 *liang* each of *sanleng* (sparganium, vinegar-processed), *ewu* (curcuma, vinegar-processed and dried), *cangzhu* (atractylodes, rice-water processed and stir-fried), and *chenpi* (aged tangerine peel, white pith removed); 1 *liang* of *houpo* (magnolia bark, ginger-juice processed); and ½ *liang* of *gancao*. Grind the first six ingredients into powder, then mix with 2 *liang* of *qingfan* and glutinous rice flour to form a paste. Form into pills. Take 50–60 pills per dose with rice-water decoction. Avoid pork, roosters, geese, beef, mutton, and other toxic foods.

**Secret Formula for Jaundice, Edema, Wine-Induced Jaundice, and Accumulated Pain**
½ *jin* of *qingfan* and 1 large cup of rice vinegar. Mix evenly in an earthenware basin and calcine over fire until dry. Combine with ½ *liang* each of *Pingwei San* and *Wu Yao Shun Qi San* (Lindera Powder to Rectify Qi). If dietary restrictions are not observed, add pot ash.

Grind into powder and form into pills with vinegar-cooked paste. For large pills (9–11 per dose), take up to 20–30 pills on an empty stomach with southern wine or ginger-salt decoction.

**Another Secret Formula: Nameless Pills for Edema**
Edema with abdominal distension and firmness, generalized swelling and pain, coughing, and labored breathing are all treated with this formula.
1 *liang* each of *chifuling* (red poria), *daji* (euphorbia, sliced—*gancao* contraindicated), and *gansui* (kan-sui); ½ *liang* of *yuanhua* (genkwa); ½ *liang* of *binglang* (areca nut); and ½ *liang* of *qingpi* (unripe tangerine peel). Grind *heicheqianniu* (black pharbitis) into powder and combine with the above. Form into *wutong*-sized pills with thin wheat-flour paste. Adjust the dosage (30 pills per dose) according to the severity of the condition.

**Decoctions for Administration:**
- **Edema:** Decoct with *haizao* (seaweed), *poguzhi* (psoralea), and *baimu* (white wood).
- **Facial swelling:** Decoct with *chenpi* (aged tangerine peel).
